[500px](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/파일:Skeletal_muscles_homo_sapiens.JPG "wikilink")(後頭前頭筋)

2 temporoparietalis [측두두정근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/측두두정근 "wikilink")(側頭頭頂筋)

3 orbicularis oculi [눈둘레근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/눈둘레근 "wikilink"), 안륜근

4 levator labii superioris [위입술올림근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/위입술올림근 "wikilink"), 상순거근

5 masticatorii(masticatory muscle) [씹기근육](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/씹기근육 "wikilink"), 저작근

6 sternocleidomastoideus [목빗근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/목빗근 "wikilink"),흉쇄유돌근(胸鎖乳突筋)

7 orbicularis oris [입둘레근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/입둘레근 "wikilink"), 구륜근

8 deltoideus [삼각근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/삼각근 "wikilink")(三角筋),어깨세모근

9 trapezius [등세모근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/등세모근 "wikilink")

10 pectoralis major[큰가슴근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/큰가슴근 "wikilink"), 대흉근

11 latissimus dorsi [넓은등근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/넓은등근 "wikilink"), 광배근

12 triceps brachii [상완세갈래근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/위팔세갈래근 "wikilink"), 상완삼두근(上腕三頭筋)

13 biceps brachii [위팔두갈래근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/위팔두갈래근 "wikilink"), 상완이두근

14 serratus anterior [앞톱니근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/앞톱니근 "wikilink"), 전방거근

15 rectus abdominis [배곧은근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/배곧은근 "wikilink"), 복직근

16 obliquus externus abdominis [배바깥빗근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/배바깥빗근 "wikilink"), 외복사근

17 tensor fascia lata [넙다리근막긴장근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/넙다리근막긴장근 "wikilink"), 대퇴근막장근

18 rectus femoris [넙다리곧은근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/넙다리곧은근 "wikilink"), 대퇴직근

19 gluteus maximus [큰볼기근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/큰볼기근 "wikilink"), 대둔근

20 pronator quadratus [네모엎침근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/네모엎침근 "wikilink"), 방형회내근

21 flexor retinaculum [굽힘근지지띠](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/굽힘근지지띠 "wikilink")

22 flexor digitorum communis [손가락굽힘근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/손가락굽힘근 "wikilink"), 총수지굴근

23 sartorius [넙다리빗근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/넙다리빗근 "wikilink"), 봉공근

24 quadratus femoris [넙다리네모근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/넙다리네모근 "wikilink"), 대퇴방형근

25 ischiocrurale [좌골하퇴근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/좌골하퇴근 "wikilink")

26 gastrocnemius muscle [장딴지근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/장딴지근 "wikilink"), 비복근

27 tibialis anterior [앞정강근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/앞정강근 "wikilink")

28 soleus [가자미근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/가자미근 "wikilink")

29 extensor retinaculum [폄근지지띠](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/폄근지지띠 "wikilink")

30 triceps surae [종아리세갈래근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/장딴지세갈래근 "wikilink") \]\]

[500px](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/파일:1105_Anterior_and_Posterior_Views_of_Muscles_enko_png.svg "wikilink")

일반적인 인간에게는 대략 640개의 [골격근](../Page/골격근.md "wikilink")이 있고, 대부분의 근육이 좌우대칭의 양측성 근육이므로 대략 320쌍의 근육을 이 문서에서 보여주고 있다. 그럼에도 불구하고, 정확한 숫자를 정하는 건 어려운데 왜냐하면 특정 근육을 단일 근육의 다른 부분으로 정의할지, 각각의 근육으로 정의할지 등의 문제가 있기 때문이다. 그래서 640개에서 850개로 근육의 숫자를 다르게 셀 수 있다.\[1\]

인체의 근육들은 [머리](../Page/머리.md "wikilink")와 [목](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/목 "wikilink")(head and neck)의 근육, [몸통](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/몸통 "wikilink")(torso or trunk)의 근육, [팔](../Page/팔.md "wikilink")(upper limbs)의 근육과 [다리](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/다리 "wikilink")(lower limbs)의 근육을 포함한 많은 분류로 나뉠 수 있다.

표의 "동작"(action)은 [해부학적 위치의](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/해부학적_위치 "wikilink") 각각의 근육의 동작을 의미한다.

이 근육들은 [해부학 용어](../Page/해부학_용어.md "wikilink")(anatomical terminology)를 사용하여 설명된다. 한국어, 한자어, 영어 용어가 섞여서 쓰이는 대한민국 [의학](../Page/의학.md "wikilink")계의 현실을 감안하여 한국어, 한자어, 영어 명칭을 모두 표기하였다. 여기에 사용된 한국어 명칭들은 [대한해부학회](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/대한해부학회 "wikilink") 사이트에서 배포하는 용어집을 따랐다.\[2\] 또한 아직도 [임상의학](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/임상의학 "wikilink") [의사](../Page/의사.md "wikilink")들이 많이 쓰는 한자어로 된 명칭은 KMLE 의학 검색 엔진\[3\]과 다국어 [위키백과](../Page/위키백과.md "wikilink") 등을 참고하였다.

[인체 해부학에서의](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/인체_해부학 "wikilink") [골격근](../Page/골격근.md "wikilink")의 목록은 아래 표와 같다. 아래 표를 보기 전에 [인체 뼈 목록](../Page/인체_뼈_목록.md "wikilink"), [위치에 대한 해부학 용어](../Page/위치에_대한_해부학_용어.md "wikilink"), [운동에 대한 해부학 용어](../Page/운동에_대한_해부학_용어.md "wikilink"), [근육에 대한 해부학 용어](../Page/근육에_대한_해부학_용어.md "wikilink") 문서를 읽으면 이해가 좀 더 쉬울 것이다.

### [안구근육](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/안구근육 "wikilink")([외안근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/외안근 "wikilink"), Extraocular muscles)

### [혀](../Page/혀.md "wikilink")

#### 바깥기원근육(외인근육, 외재근, Extrinsic muscles)

| 근육                                                                             | Origin                                                                                                                                                                             | Insertion                                                                                                                               | Artery                                                                    | Nerve                                                                                                                                                       | Action                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    | 대항근                                                                            |
| ------------------------------------------------------------------------------ | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------- | ----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | ----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------ |
| [턱끝혀근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/턱끝혀근 "wikilink")(genioglossus muscle)     | Superior part of mental spine of [mandible](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/human_mandible "wikilink") ([symphysis menti](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/symphysis_menti "wikilink")) | Dorsum of [tongue](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/tongue "wikilink") and body of [hyoid](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/hyoid "wikilink") | [Lingual artery](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lingual_artery "wikilink") | [hypoglossal nerve](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/hypoglossal_nerve "wikilink")                                                                             | Complex – Inferior fibers protrude the [tongue](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/tongue "wikilink"), middle fibers depress the [tongue](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/tongue "wikilink"), and its superior fibers draw the tip back and down |                                                                                |
| [목뿔혀근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/목뿔혀근 "wikilink")(hyoglossus muscle)       | [목뿔뼈](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/목뿔뼈 "wikilink")(hyoid bone)                                                                                                                    | side of the tongue                                                                                                                      |                                                                           | [hypoglossal nerve](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/hypoglossal_nerve "wikilink")                                                                             | depresses tongue                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |                                                                                |
| [작은뿔혀근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/작은뿔혀근 "wikilink")(chondroglossus muscle) | [lesser cornu](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/lesser_cornu "wikilink") and body of the [hyoid bone](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/hyoid_bone "wikilink")                            | intrinsic muscular fibers of the [tongue](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/tongue "wikilink")                                              |                                                                           | [hypoglossal nerve](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/hypoglossal_nerve "wikilink")                                                                             | depresses tongue (some consider this muscle to be part of [hyoglossus](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/hyoglossus "wikilink"))                                                                                                              |                                                                                |
| [붓혀근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/붓혀근 "wikilink")(styloglossus muscle)       | [Styloid process of temporal bone](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/styloid_process_\(temporal\) "wikilink")                                                                          | tongue                                                                                                                                  |                                                                           | [Hypoglossal nerve](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hypoglossal_nerve "wikilink")                                                                             | elevates and retracts tongue                                                                                                                                                                                                              | [턱끝혀근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/턱끝혀근 "wikilink")(genioglossus)의 아래와 중간 섬유 |
| [입천장혀근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/입천장혀근 "wikilink")(Palatoglossus muscle)  | [palatine aponeurosis](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/palatine_aponeurosis "wikilink")                                                                                              | [tongue](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/tongue "wikilink")                                                                               |                                                                           | [vagus nerve](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/vagus_nerve "wikilink") and cranial [accessory nerve](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/accessory_nerve "wikilink") | raising the back part of the [tongue](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/tongue "wikilink")                                                                                                                                                    |                                                                                |
|                                                                                |                                                                                                                                                                                    |                                                                                                                                         |                                                                           |                                                                                                                                                             |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |                                                                                |

#### 자체기원근육(내인근육, 내재근, Intrinsic muscles)

| 근육                                                                                      | Origin                                                                                                                                                                           | Insertion                                                              | Artery | Nerve                                                                           | Action                                                   | 대항근 |
| --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------- | ------ | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------- | --- |
| [혀위세로근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/혀위세로근 "wikilink")(superior longitudinal muscle)   | close to the [epiglottis](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/epiglottis "wikilink"), from the [median fibrous septum](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/median_fibrous_septum "wikilink") | edges of the tongue                                                    |        | [hypoglossal nerve](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/hypoglossal_nerve "wikilink") | shortens, turns tip upward, turns lateral margins upward |     |
| [혀가로근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/혀가로근 "wikilink")(transverse muscle)                | [median fibrous septum](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/median_fibrous_septum "wikilink")                                                                                          | sides of the [tongue](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/tongue "wikilink") |        | [hypoglossal nerve](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/hypoglossal_nerve "wikilink") | narrows and elongates                                    |     |
| [혀아래세로근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/혀아래세로근 "wikilink")(inferior longitudinal muscle) | root of the tongue                                                                                                                                                               | apex of the tongue                                                     |        | [Hypoglossal nerve](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hypoglossal_nerve "wikilink") | shortens, retracts, pulls tip downward                   |     |
| [혀수직근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/혀수직근 "wikilink")(vertical muscle)                  | dorsum of tongue                                                                                                                                                                 | inferior surface borders of tongue                                     |        | [hypoglossal nerve](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/hypoglossal_nerve "wikilink") | flattens                                                 |     |
|                                                                                         |                                                                                                                                                                                  |                                                                        |        |                                                                                 |                                                          |     |

### [물렁입천장](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/물렁입천장 "wikilink")([연구개](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/연구개 "wikilink"), Soft palate)

| 근육                                                                                      | Origin                                                                                                                                                        | Insertion                                                                                                                        | Artery                                                                                                                                                               | Nerve                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             | Action                                                                                                                                                                                                                   | 대항근 |
| --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ | --- |
| [입천장올림근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/입천장올림근 "wikilink")(levator veli palatini muscle) | [temporal bone](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/temporal_bone "wikilink"), [Eustachian tube](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/Eustachian_tube "wikilink")          | [palatine aponeurosis](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/palatine_aponeurosis "wikilink")                                            | [facial artery](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/facial_artery "wikilink")                                                                                              | [vagus nerve](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/vagus_nerve "wikilink")                                                                                                                                                                               | Aids in [swallowing](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/swallowing "wikilink") by elevating the [soft palate](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/soft_palate "wikilink")                                                           |     |
| [입천장긴장근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/입천장긴장근 "wikilink")(tensor veli palatini muscle)  | medial pterygoid plate of the sphenoid bone                                                                                                                   |                                                                                                                                  | [medial pterygoid](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medial_pterygoid_nerve "wikilink") of [mandibular nerve](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/mandibular_nerve "wikilink") | Aids in [swallowing](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/swallowing "wikilink") by controlling the [tension](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/tension_\(mechanics\) "wikilink") of the [soft palate](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/soft_palate "wikilink") |                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |     |
| [목젖근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/목젖근 "wikilink")(musculus uvulae)                    | [hard palate](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/hard_palate "wikilink")                                                                                           |                                                                                                                                  | [pharyngeal plexus](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pharyngeal_plexus_of_vagus_nerve "wikilink")                                                                       | Moves and changes shape of the [uvula](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/uvula "wikilink")                                                                                                                                                            |                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |     |
| [입천장혀근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/입천장혀근 "wikilink")(Palatoglossus muscle)           | [palatine aponeurosis](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/palatine_aponeurosis "wikilink")                                                                         | [tongue](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/tongue "wikilink")                                                                        |                                                                                                                                                                      | [vagus nerve](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/vagus_nerve "wikilink") and cranial [accessory nerve](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/accessory_nerve "wikilink")                                                                                       | Aids in [respiration](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/breathing "wikilink") by raising the back part of the [tongue](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/tongue "wikilink")                                                      |     |
| [입천장인두근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/입천장인두근 "wikilink")(palatopharyngeus muscle)      | [palatine aponeurosis](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/palatine_aponeurosis "wikilink") and [hard palate](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/hard_palate "wikilink") | upper border of [thyroid cartilage](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/thyroid_cartilage "wikilink") (blends with constrictor fibers) | [facial artery](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/facial_artery "wikilink")                                                                                              | [vagus nerve](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/vagus_nerve "wikilink") and [cranial accessory nerve](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/Accessory_nerve "wikilink")                                                                                       | Aids in [respiration](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/breathing "wikilink") by pulling the [pharynx](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/human_pharynx "wikilink") and [larynx](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/larynx "wikilink") |     |
|                                                                                         |                                                                                                                                                               |                                                                                                                                  |                                                                                                                                                                      |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |     |

## [목](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/목 "wikilink") 부위

### 빗장뼈 부위(Clavicular)

<tr class="odd">
<td><p><a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/넓은목근" title="wikilink">넓은목근</a>(Platysma)</p></td>
<td><p>inferior <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/빗장뼈" title="wikilink">빗장뼈</a>(clavicle) and fascia of chest</p></td>
<td><p><a href="../Page/아래턱뼈.md" title="wikilink">아래턱뼈</a>(mandible)</p></td>
<td><p>branches of the <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/submental_artery" title="wikilink">submental artery</a> and <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/suprascapular_artery" title="wikilink">suprascapular artery</a></p></td>
<td><p><a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/cervical_branch_of_the_facial_nerve" title="wikilink">cervical branch of the facial nerve</a> (CN VII)</p></td>
<td><p>Draws the corners of the <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/mouth" title="wikilink">mouth</a> <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/inferiorly" title="wikilink">inferiorly</a> and widens it (as in expressions of sadness and fright). Also draws the <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/skin" title="wikilink">skin</a> of the <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/neck" title="wikilink">neck</a> <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anatomical_terms_of_location#Superior_and_inferior" title="wikilink">superiorly</a> when <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/teeth" title="wikilink">teeth</a> are clenched</p></td>
<td><p><a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/깨물근" title="wikilink">깨물근</a>(Masseter muscle), <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/관자근" title="wikilink">관자근</a>(Temporalis muscle)</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="even">
<td><p><a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/목빗근" title="wikilink">목빗근</a>(Sternocleidomastoid muscle)</p></td>
<td><p><a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/manubrium_sterni" title="wikilink">manubrium sterni</a>, medial portion of the <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/빗장뼈" title="wikilink">빗장뼈</a>(clavicle)</p></td>
<td><p><a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/mastoid_process_of_the_temporal_bone" title="wikilink">mastoid process of the temporal bone</a>, <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/superior_nuchal_line" title="wikilink">superior nuchal line</a></p></td>
<td><p><a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/occipital_artery" title="wikilink">occipital artery</a> and the <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/superior_thyroid_artery" title="wikilink">superior thyroid artery</a></p></td>
<td><p>motor: <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/accessory_nerve" title="wikilink">accessory nerve</a><br />
sensory: <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/cervical_plexus" title="wikilink">cervical plexus</a></p></td>
<td><p>Acting alone, tilts head to its own side and rotates it so the face is turned towards the opposite side. Acting together, flexes the neck, raises the sternum and assists in forced inspiration.</p></td>

| 목                                                                                            | Origin                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   | Insertion                                                                                                                                                                         | Artery | Nerve                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  | Action                                                                                                                                                                                                              | 대항근 |

| [목긴근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/목긴근 "wikilink")(Longus colli muscle)                     | Transverse processes of C-3 - C-6                                                                                                                                                                                                        | Anterior arch of [atlas](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/atlas "wikilink")                                                                                                          |        | [C2](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/cervical_spinal_nerve_2 "wikilink"), [C3](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/cervical_spinal_nerve_3 "wikilink"), [C4](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/cervical_spinal_nerve_4 "wikilink"), [C5](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/cervical_spinal_nerve_5 "wikilink"), [C6](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/cervical_spinal_nerve_6 "wikilink") | Flexes the neck and head                                                                                                                                                                                            |     |
| [머리긴근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/머리긴근 "wikilink")(Longus capitis muscle)                 | anterior tubercles of the [transverse processes](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/transverse_processes "wikilink") of the third, fourth, fifth, and sixth [cervical vertebrae](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/cervical_vertebrae "wikilink") | [basilar](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/basilar_artery "wikilink") part of the [occipital bone](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/occipital_bone "wikilink")                          |        | [C1](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/cervical_spinal_nerve_1 "wikilink"), [C2](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/cervical_spinal_nerve_2 "wikilink"), [C3](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/cervical_spinal_nerve_3 "wikilink")/[C4](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/cervical_spinal_nerve_4 "wikilink")                                                                          | [flexion](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/flexion "wikilink") of [neck](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/neck "wikilink") at [atlanto-occipital joint](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/atlanto-occipital_joint "wikilink") |     |
| [앞머리곧은근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/앞머리곧은근 "wikilink")(Rectus capitis anterior muscle)    | [atlas](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/Atlas_\(anatomy\) "wikilink")                                                                                                                                                                      | [occipital bone](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/occipital_bone "wikilink")                                                                                                         |        | [C1](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/cervical_spinal_nerve_1 "wikilink")                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 | [flexion](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/flexion "wikilink") of [neck](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/neck "wikilink") at [atlanto-occipital joint](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/atlanto-occipital_joint "wikilink") |     |

| ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | --------------------- | --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | --- |
| [작은뒤머리곧은근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/작은뒤머리곧은근 "wikilink")(Rectus capitis posterior minor muscle) | the tubercle on the posterior arch of the [atlas](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/Atlas_\(anatomy\) "wikilink") (C1)                                                                                                       | the medial part of the [inferior nuchal line](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/inferior_nuchal_line "wikilink") of the [occipital bone](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/occipital_bone "wikilink") and the surface between it and the [foramen magnum](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/foramen_magnum "wikilink") |                       | a branch of the dorsal primary division of the [suboccipital nerve](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/suboccipital_nerve "wikilink")                                                                                                                    | [extends](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/extension_\(kinesiology\) "wikilink") the head at the neck, but is now considered to be more of a sensory organ than a muscle |     |
| [큰뒤머리곧은근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/큰뒤머리곧은근 "wikilink")(Rectus capitis posterior major muscle)   | [spinous process](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/spinous_process "wikilink") of the [axis](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/Axis_\(anatomy\) "wikilink") ([C2](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/cervical_vertebrae "wikilink")) | [inferior nucheal line](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/inferior_nucheal_line "wikilink") of the [occipital bone](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/occipital_bone "wikilink")                                                                                                                                   |                       | [Dorsal ramus](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dorsal_ramus_of_spinal_nerve "wikilink") of [C1](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/cervical_spinal_nerve_1 "wikilink") ([suboccipital nerve](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/suboccipital_nerve "wikilink")) |                                                                                                                                                                       |     |
| [머리반가시근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/머리반가시근 "wikilink")(semispinalis capitis muscle)               | articular processes of C4-C6; transverse processes of C7 and T1-T7                                                                                                                                                       | occipital bone between the superior and inferior nuchal lines                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |                       | greater occipital nerve                                                                                                                                                                                                                             | Extension of the head                                                                                                                                                 |     |
| [머리가장긴근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/머리가장긴근 "wikilink")(longissimus capitis muscle)                | articular processes of C4-C7; transverse processes of T1-T5                                                                                                                                                              | posterior margin of the mastoid process                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    | lateral sacral artery | posterior branch of spinal nerve                                                                                                                                                                                                                    | Laterally: Flex the head and neck to the same side. Bilaterally: Extend the vertebral column.                                                                         |     |
| [머리널판근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/머리널판근 "wikilink")(Splenius capitis muscle)                     | ligamentum nuchae, spinous processes of [C7](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/cervical_vertebrae "wikilink")-[T6](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/thoracic_vertebrae "wikilink")                                              | Mastoid process                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |                       | [C3](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/cervical_spinal_nerve_3 "wikilink"), [C4](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/cervical_spinal_nerve_4 "wikilink")                                                                                                      | Extend, rotate, and laterally flex the head                                                                                                                           |     |
| [위머리빗근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/위머리빗근 "wikilink")(Obliquus capitis superior muscle)            | [lateral mass of atlas](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/lateral_mass_of_atlas "wikilink")                                                                                                                                  | lateral half of the [inferior nuchal line](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/inferior_nuchal_line "wikilink")                                                                                                                                                                                                  |                       | [suboccipital nerve](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/suboccipital_nerve "wikilink")                                                                                                                                                                   |                                                                                                                                                                       |     |

<td><p><a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/배가로근" title="wikilink">배가로근</a>(Transversus abdominis muscle)</p></td>

<td><p>inserts into the <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/pubis_(bone)" title="wikilink">pubic tubercle</a> via the conjoint tendon, also known as the <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/falx_inguinalis" title="wikilink">falx inguinalis</a></p></td>
<td></td>
<td><p><a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/intercostal_nerve" title="wikilink">intercostal nerves</a> <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/thoracic_spinal_nerve_7" title="wikilink">T7</a>, <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/thoracic_spinal_nerve_8" title="wikilink">T8</a>, <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/thoracic_spinal_nerve_9" title="wikilink">T9</a>, <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/thoracic_spinal_nerve_10" title="wikilink">T10</a>, <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/thoracic_spinal_nerve_11" title="wikilink">T11</a>, <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/subcostal_nerve" title="wikilink">subcostal nerve</a> (<a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/thoracic_spinal_nerve_12" title="wikilink">T12</a>), <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/iliohypogastric_nerve" title="wikilink">iliohypogastric nerve</a>, <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/ilioinguinal_nerve" title="wikilink">ilioinguinal nerve</a>, <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/genitofemoral_nerve" title="wikilink">genitofemoral nerve</a></p></td>
<td><p>compress the ribs and viscera, providing thoracic and pelvic stability</p></td>
<td></td>

<td><p>perineal branch of the <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/pudendal_nerve" title="wikilink">pudendal nerve</a> (<a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/sacral_spinal_nerve_2" title="wikilink">S2</a>, <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/sacral_spinal_nerve_3" title="wikilink">S3</a>, <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/sacral_spinal_nerve_4" title="wikilink">S4</a>)</p></td>
<td><p>Constricts urethra, maintain urinary continence</p></td>
<td></td>

<td><p><a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rib" title="wikilink">costal</a> aspect of <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/medial_margin_of_the_scapula" title="wikilink">medial margin of the scapula</a></p></td>
<td><p><a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/lateral_thoracic_artery" title="wikilink">lateral thoracic artery</a> (upper part), <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/thoracodorsal_artery" title="wikilink">thoracodorsal artery</a> (lower part)</p></td>
<td><p><a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/long_thoracic_nerve" title="wikilink">long thoracic nerve</a> (from roots of <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/brachial_plexus" title="wikilink">brachial plexus</a> <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/cervical_spinal_nerve_5" title="wikilink">C5</a>, <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/cervical_spinal_nerve_6" title="wikilink">C6</a>, <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/cervical_spinal_nerve_7" title="wikilink">C7</a>)</p></td>
<td><p><a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/protract" title="wikilink">protract</a> and stabilize <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/어깨뼈" title="wikilink">어깨뼈</a>(scapula), assists in upward rotation</p></td>
<td><p><a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/큰마름근" title="wikilink">큰마름근</a>(Rhomboid major muscle), <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/작은마름근" title="wikilink">작은마름근</a>(Rhomboid minor muscle), <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/등세모근" title="wikilink">등세모근</a>(<a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/승모근" title="wikilink">승모근</a>, Trapezius muscle)</p></td>

<tr class="even">
<td><p><a href="../Page/팔꿈치근.md" title="wikilink">팔꿈치근</a>(anconeus muscle)</p></td>
<td><p><a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/위팔뼈의_가쪽위관절융기" title="wikilink">위팔뼈의 가쪽위관절융기</a>(Lateral epicondyle of the humerus)</p></td>
<td><p><a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/팔꿈치머리" title="wikilink">팔꿈치머리</a>(olecranon) 돌기의 가쪽과 <a href="../Page/자뼈.md" title="wikilink">자뼈</a>(ulna) 뒷면의 위쪽</p></td>
<td><p><a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/깊은위팔동맥" title="wikilink">깊은위팔동맥</a>(Deep brachial artery, Profunda brachii artery), <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/되돌이뼈사이동맥" title="wikilink">되돌이뼈사이동맥</a>(recurrent interosseous artery)</p></td>
<td><p><a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/노신경" title="wikilink">노신경</a>(radial nerve: <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/일곱째_목신경" title="wikilink">일곱째 목신경</a>(cervical spinal nerve 7, C7), <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/여덟째_목신경" title="wikilink">여덟째 목신경</a>(cervical spinal nerve 8, C8), <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/첫째_가슴신경" title="wikilink">첫째 가슴신경</a>(thoracic spinal nerve 1, T1))</p></td>
<td><p>partly blended in with the <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/위팔세갈래근" title="wikilink">위팔세갈래근</a>(triceps), which it assists in <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/extension_(kinesiology)" title="wikilink">extension</a> of the <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/forearm" title="wikilink">forearm</a>. Stabilises the elbow and <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/Abduction_(kinesiology)" title="wikilink">abducts</a> the ulna during <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/pronation" title="wikilink">pronation</a>.</p></td>
<td></td>
</tr>

<td></td>

</table>

<td><p><a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/deep_branch_of_ulnar_nerve" title="wikilink">deep branch of ulnar nerve</a></p></td>
<td><p>Abduction of <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/little_finger" title="wikilink">little finger</a></p></td>
<td></td>
</tr>
<tr class="even">
<td><p><a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/짧은새끼굽힘근" title="wikilink">짧은새끼굽힘근</a>(Flexor digiti minimi brevis muscle)</p></td>
<td><p><a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/hamate_bone" title="wikilink">hamate bone</a></p></td>
<td><p><a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/little_finger" title="wikilink">little finger</a></p></td>
<td><p><a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/ulnar_artery" title="wikilink">ulnar artery</a></p></td>

<td><p><a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/새끼폄근" title="wikilink">새끼폄근</a>(extensor digiti minimi muscle)</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="odd">
<td><p><a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/새끼맞섬근" title="wikilink">새끼맞섬근</a>(opponens digiti minimi muscle)</p></td>
<td><p>Hook of <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/hamate" title="wikilink">hamate</a> and <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/flexor_retinaculum_of_the_hand" title="wikilink">flexor retinaculum</a></p></td>

<td><p><a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/ulnar_artery" title="wikilink">ulnar artery</a></p></td>

<td><p>Draws <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fifth_metacarpal_bone" title="wikilink">5th metacarpal</a> anteriorly and rotates it, bringing little finger (5th digit) into opposition with thumb</p></td>
<td></td>

<td><p>Works in concert with gluteus medius: <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/anatomical_terms_of_location" title="wikilink">abduction</a> of the hip; preventing <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/anatomical_terms_of_location" title="wikilink">adduction</a> of the hip. Medial rotation of thigh.</p></td>

#### 넓적다리 뒷부분/[넙다리뒤근육](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/넙다리뒤근육 "wikilink")(hamstring, 슬와근, 오금)

| 근육                                                                                                                                          | Origin                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       | Insertion                                                                                                                                                                                      | Artery                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   | Nerve                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   | Action                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               | 대항근                                                                                                                                           |
| ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| [넙다리두갈래근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/넙다리두갈래근 "wikilink")([대퇴이두근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/대퇴이두근 "wikilink"), biceps femoris muscle) | 긴갈래(long head): [궁둥뼈결절](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/궁둥뼈결절 "wikilink")(Ischial tuberosity, tuberosity of the ischium), 짧은갈래(short head): [넙다리뼈](../Page/넙다리뼈.md "wikilink")(femur)의 [거친선](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/거친선 "wikilink")(linea aspera)\[10\] | [정강뼈의 가쪽관절융기](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/정강뼈의_가쪽관절융기 "wikilink")(Lateral condyle of tibia)의 뒷면과 관절로 연결된 [종아리뼈머리](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/종아리뼈머리 "wikilink")(head of the fibula)\[11\] | [아래볼기동맥](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/아래볼기동맥 "wikilink")(inferior gluteal artery), [관통동맥](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/관통동맥 "wikilink")(perforating arteries), [오금동맥](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/오금동맥 "wikilink")(popliteal artery) | 긴갈래(long head): [궁둥신경](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/궁둥신경 "wikilink")(sciatic nerve)의 [안쪽](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/표준_해부학적_위치 "wikilink")([정강뼈](../Page/정강뼈.md "wikilink")쪽) 부분, 짧은갈래(short head): [궁둥신경](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/궁둥신경 "wikilink")(sciatic nerve)의 [가쪽](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/표준_해부학적_위치 "wikilink")([종아리뼈](../Page/종아리뼈.md "wikilink")쪽(common fibular)) 부분(\[12\] | [무릎관절](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/무릎관절 "wikilink")(knee joint) [구부리기](../Page/운동에_대한_해부학_용어.md "wikilink")(flexion), 무릎이 구부러져 있을 때 무릎의 다리를 [바깥쪽으로 회전하기](../Page/운동에_대한_해부학_용어.md "wikilink")(lateral rotation), [엉덩관절](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/엉덩관절 "wikilink")(hip joint) [펴기](../Page/운동에_대한_해부학_용어.md "wikilink")(Extension)(긴갈래만)\[13\] | [넙다리네모근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/넙다리네모근 "wikilink")([대퇴사두근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/대퇴사두근 "wikilink"), Quadriceps femoris muscle) |
| [반힘줄근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/반힘줄근 "wikilink")(semitendinosus muscle)                                                                | tuberosity of the ischium\[14\]                                                                                                                                                                                                                              | [pes anserinus](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/pes_anserinus_\(leg\) "wikilink")                                                                                                                | [inferior gluteal artery](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/inferior_gluteal_artery "wikilink"), [perforating arteries](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/perforating_arteries "wikilink")                                                       | [sciatic](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/sciatic_nerve "wikilink")\[15\] ([tibial](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/tibial_nerve "wikilink"), [L5](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/lumbar_spinal_nerve_5 "wikilink"), [S1](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/sacral_spinal_nerve_1 "wikilink"), [S2](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/sacral_spinal_nerve_2 "wikilink"))                                             | flexes knee, extends hip joint, [medially rotates](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/medially_rotates "wikilink") leg at knee\[16\]                                                                                                                                                                                                                      | [넙다리네모근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/넙다리네모근 "wikilink")(Quadriceps femoris muscle)                                                          |
| [반막근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/반막근 "wikilink")(semimembranosus muscle)                                                                 | tuberosity of the ischium\[17\]                                                                                                                                                                                                                              | Medial surface of [정강뼈](../Page/정강뼈.md "wikilink")(tibia)\[18\]                                                                                                                                | [profunda femoris](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/profunda_femoris "wikilink"), [gluteal artery](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gluteal_artery_\(disambiguation\) "wikilink")                                                              | [sciatic nerve](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/sciatic_nerve "wikilink")\[19\]                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           | flexes knee, extends hip joint, medially rotates leg at knee\[20\]                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   | [넙다리네모근](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/넙다리네모근 "wikilink")(Quadriceps femoris muscle)                                                          |

<td><p>lateral supracondylar ridge of <a href="../Page/넙다리뼈.md" title="wikilink">넙다리뼈</a>(femur) above lateral head of gastrocnemius</p></td>
<td><p><a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/tendo_calcaneus" title="wikilink">tendo calcaneus</a> (medial side, deep to <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/gastrocnemius" title="wikilink">gastrocnemius</a> tendon)</p></td>
<td><p><a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/sural_arteries" title="wikilink">sural arteries</a></p></td>
<td><p><a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/tibial_nerve" title="wikilink">tibial nerve</a></p></td>
<td><p><a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/Plantar_flexes" title="wikilink">Plantar flexes</a> <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/foot" title="wikilink">foot</a> and flexes <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/knee" title="wikilink">knee</a></p></td>
<td><p><a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/앞정강근" title="wikilink">앞정강근</a>(Tibialis anterior muscle)</p></td>
